</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">expansion of 10 basis points --</font></div><div style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">-- Company declares quarterly cash dividend of $0.80 per share, a 10% increase over the equivalent quarterly rate last year --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">NEW YORK; Mar. 19, 2020 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE: ACN) reported financial results for the second quarter of fiscal 2020, ended Feb. 29, 2020, with revenues of $11.1&#160;billion, an increase of 7% in U.S. dollars and 8% in local currency over the same period last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Diluted earnings per share were $1.91, a 10% increase from the second quarter last year.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating income was $1.49 billion, a 7% increase over the same period last year, and operating margin was 13.4%, an expansion of 10 basis points.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">New bookings for the quarter were $14.2 billion, with consulting bookings of $7.2&#160;billion and outsourcing bookings of $7.0&#160;billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Julie Sweet, Accenture&#8217;s chief executive officer, said, &#8220;The world is now facing a global health crisis and significant disruption in the global economy.&#160;I am incredibly proud of how our leadership team and all our people have rallied to ensure the safety and well-being of each other while continuing to serve our clients at this time of great need. We exited the first half of our fiscal year in a clear position of strength &#8212; delivering excellent results, gaining significant market share and continuing to successfully execute our growth strategy. As we move forward, we will focus on helping our clients navigate and succeed in this uncertain period and continue to invest in our business and our people for the long term.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Financial Review</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Revenues for the second quarter of fiscal 2020 were $11.14&#160;billion, compared with $10.45&#160;billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2019, an increase of 7% in U.S. dollars and 8% in local currency, at the top end of the company&#8217;s guided range of $10.85&#160;billion to $11.15 billion. The foreign-exchange impact for the quarter was approximately negative 1%, consistent with the assumption provided in the company&#8217;s first-quarter earnings release. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; The $0.18 increase in EPS reflects:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9642;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">a $0.14&#160;increase from higher revenue and operating results; and  </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9642;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">a $0.04 increase from higher non-operating income. </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 30.2%, compared with 29.2% for the second quarter last year. Selling, general and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses for the quarter were $1.87&#160;billion, or 16.8% of revenues, compared with $1.67&#160;billion, or 16.0% of revenues, for the second quarter last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating income for the quarter increased 7%, to $1.49 billion, or 13.4% of revenues, compared with $1.39 billion, or 13.3% of revenues, for the second quarter of fiscal 2019.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the quarter was 17.1%, compared with 17.1% for the second quarter last year. </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net income for the quarter was $1.25 billion, a 10% increase from $1.14 billion for the second quarter last year.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $1.53 billion and property and equipment additions were $165&#160;million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $1.37&#160;billion for the quarter. For the same period last year, operating cash flow was $1.36 billion; property and equipment additions were $140&#160;million; and free cash flow was $1.22 billion. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 39 days at Feb. 29, 2020, compared with 40 days at Aug. 31, 2019 and 40 days at Feb. 28, 2019. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at Feb. 29, 2020 was $5.4&#160;billion, compared with $6.1&#160;billion at Aug. 31, 2019. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">New Bookings</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">New bookings for the second quarter were $14.2&#160;billion and reflect a negative 1% foreign-currency impact compared with new bookings in the second quarter last year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9642;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Consulting new bookings were $7.2&#160;billion, or 50% of total new bookings.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; On Feb. 14, 2020, a quarterly cash dividend of $0.80 per share was paid to shareholders of record at the close of business on Jan. 16, 2020. These cash dividend payments totaled $511 million, bringing dividend payments for the year to date to $1.02&#160;billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Accenture plc has declared another quarterly cash dividend of $0.80 per share for shareholders of record at the close of business on Apr. 16, 2020. This dividend is payable on May 15, 2020. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">In fiscal 2019, the company paid semi-annual cash dividends of $1.46&#160;per share, equivalent to quarterly payments of $0.73 per share. The quarterly dividend of $0.80 per share this year represents a 10% increase over the equivalent quarterly rate in fiscal 2019. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase Activity</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">During the second quarter of fiscal 2020, Accenture repurchased or redeemed 4.7&#160;million shares, including 2.7 million shares repurchased in the open market, for a total of $970 million. This brings Accenture&#8217;s total share repurchases and redemptions for the first half of fiscal 2020 to 8.5 million shares, including 6.0 million shares repurchased in the open market, for a total of $1.70 billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Accenture&#8217;s total remaining share repurchase authority at Feb. 29, 2020 was approximately $2.5&#160;billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">At Feb. 29, 2020, Accenture had approximately 637&#160;million total shares outstanding.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Business Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">The coronavirus (COVID-19) crisis is rapidly evolving and has created a significant amount of uncertainty. The extent to which this impacts Accenture&#8217;s business, operations, and financial results, including the duration and magnitude of such impact, will depend on numerous factors that the company may not be able to accurately predict, including those discussed in the Risk Factors set forth in Accenture&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 10-K and second quarter Form 10-Q filings with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div Financial results &#8220;in local currency&#8221; are calculated by restating current-period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior-year period&#8217;s foreign-currency exchange rates. Accenture&#8217;s management believes providing investors with this information gives additional insights into Accenture&#8217;s results of operations. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that the non-GAAP financial measures herein are useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP. Accenture provides full-year revenue guidance on a local-currency basis and not in U.S. dollars because the impact of foreign exchange rate fluctuations could vary significantly from the company&#8217;s stated assumptions. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:8pt;color:#4e586a;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Except for the historical information and discussions contained herein, statements in this news release may constitute forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
